< Review>
I use the post office regularly, and since I have been in La Habra I have had numerous problems with this post office and some of the carriers. Today I had a packaged "Out for Delivery" per tracking info.  I met the Postal Carrier at the apartment's mailboxes, just in case there were no large package mailboxes, and so the carrier would not need to go to my apartment. He said he didn't have a package for me, if so I would have a key in my box.  I didn't.  I then asked if he would check the large mailboxes and he wouldn't.  Got back to my apartment and tracking said package was delivered. Nothing there. This is the 4th time I've had confirmation saying a package was delivered, when the other times it was still on the truck or misdirected.

I also schedule pick-ups.  A service they offer.  I had on 5 occasions, no one show for the pick up. I'm the last stop on the route, so by the time I realize I have been missed, it's pretty much to late to call the post office.  I have caught them twice and they made a trip to pick up my items. When checking the status online they marked items as picked-up, when they definitely did not come by.

I've had First Class packages picked up on Tuesday, but not showing up on tracking until Thursday morning.  I know it takes a bit to update, but the info going out is saying the post office received the item on Thursday, not Tuesday when they took possession.

In this day and age with everything linked, it is necessary for the post office to be accurate.  New ordered Cell phones are turned on when delivered, with old ones disconnected as soon as delivery confirmation is received.  Ebay holds funds for some sellers based on if packages are shipped/ picked up/delivered within certain time frames. Updates are sent via automated emails, texts and phone calls. This is based on the USPS tracking info.

I've been doing online sales for 15 years, and have never had a problem remotely close to all I have had in La Habra.  Next time I shall give my thoughts on the counter service.  I had an employee of the La Habra Post Office even recommend I use a different office. WOW!  ADDITIONAL COMMENTS ADDED ON 9/1/15 The site would not let me do another review, so I am adding to my previous.  A few weeks back, tracking showed packaged delivered.  No package there, no key for parcel box (I'm in an apartment).  Found out a week later the key was in an empty PO box next to mine that they keep a few supplies in. Today tracking shows a package out for delivery at 9:35am. No package here.  Still listed as out for delivery, so I'm assuming it was left on the vehicle.  Hope it arrives tomorrow.</Review>

< Text>
Disclaimer: I was not given incentive or benefit in any form whatsoever to write this review. This review is written from my personal experience and perspective from my visit to the restaurant as a paying customer.

First things first, this spot is under new ownership as of Oct '19. Upon a single glance, the prices are quite reasonable for a sushi restaurant and the menu has a new nicely balanced mix of fresh contemporary and classic dishes. The appetizers are absolutely amazing. You get an entire experience from the start. This is a spot for any crowd or crew that appreciates high quality sushi. Regardless your age, gender or ethnic group, if you enjoy sushi, this place is definitely worth your time and money. The service is also top notch. The staff will take your order quite promptly and will bring out your starting side dishes nearly as soon. They will also clear all empty and unused bowls and trash out of the way in an as undisruptive manner as possible upon request or upon their discretion. The fish quality is just out of this world. They are all incredibly fresh and have that melt-in-your-mouth quality that avid sushi consumers crave and seek. The soba is definitely worth a try for those who love cold noodles. The noodles are cooked to perfection and presentation is also nice. The dipping sauce/soup for the noodles is very delicious and refreshing as well. Also the flavor is different (and in my opinion, better) than the generic store-bought type of dipping sauce/soup that you find every other sushi restaurant using for their soba. For those of you who read up to this point, you read this long for a reason and i hope this review gave you a reason to visit New Sho Gun Sushi. You won't regret it. My family and i loved our dining experience here.<//Text>

< Review>
The NEW Shogun restaurant (opened under new ownership as of Oct. 2019) is super delish!!! It is a small restaurant, but it is nice and organized neatly on top of being very clean. The food was amazing; I ordered the soba/sushi set and the sushi was great. The highlight of my meal was definitely the soba though! The noodles were fresh and light matched with a sweet, yet savory dipping sauce. You can add wasabi, thinly sliced green onions and the radish according to season the sauce however spicy you want it. I am not lying when I say it is the best soba I have ever eaten ðŸ¤¤!!!

Overall experience:
Parking - Valet....believe it's $2?
Price - It is a new ownership, but it isn't as expensive as the old Shogun.
Food - 5 out of 5
Space - it is a tiny spot. There are two small private rooms (max. 4 i think) and the rest are pretty much the same. I can't remember if there is bar seating.
Service - was excellent~
Recommend - to anyone and everyone in KTOWN LA who wants to eat some yummy sushi! ðŸ‘ðŸ‘ðŸ‘ðŸ‘ðŸ‘<//Review>

<Rating>5< /Rating>< Text>
Great skate park. There are disignated times for skateboards, scooters or bikes. specially when it's not crowded is the best time. We show up at random times so I can't say when it's really a good time. If they ask if you have a membership, I just found out it means your waiver/paperwork you signed in the past will be in there book records there at the check in desk. They check for you name & yes, it's still free. Get signed up with their waiver/paperwork & you'll be considered a member for anytime you come back in the future. Enjoy!</Text>

< review>
One of the most delicious Thai Food ever in Bay Area Hands Down !! Being one of many old Thai Delicacies in Berkeley, this place has been consistently serving delicious and quality Thai Foods.
Since new owners took this place, the quality of food, service and overall ambience has definitely been improved way much better.
Yellow Chicken Curry has been one of my favorites because of the coconut milk that accentuate the deliciousness of the dish.
Roasted Duck Curry is also one of my absolute favourite, the duck meat is so juicy and tender.
100% Recommended.< /review>

<Pictures>None<//Pictures><user_name>Ted Eby<//user_name><resp>None< /resp><userid>103646483219223289289<//userid><review>I had a very pleasant lunch here. The service was fast, attentive, and friendly. I ordered a basil chicken rice plate, spicy and a hot Thai tea. First off, the rice was the best I've had in Berkeley. It was cooked to the point where it is soft, but not mushy. Also, there was a slight jasmine flavor that made the rice enjoyable to eat on its own, opposed to being strictly a starch to mop up left over sauce with. The basil chicken was flavorful; the meat and vegetables were fresh. The Thai hot tea managed to translate the flavor of Thai iced tea without all of the calories from the cream (free refills too). The only thing I can criticize is that my dish wasn't spicy enough, but that may be due to my love for painfully spicy food. I would highly recommend walking a few extra blocks from downtown Berkeley to have the opportunity to enjoy this gem.< /review><gmap_id>0x80857ea1c8988d17:0xece1a0dfa7274ed3</gmap_id><Rating>5</Rating><Date>1375304270431< /Date></record></dataset><record>
